$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / Do_While_Loops_Coutning1

::Do While Loops Counting Level 1 #000::
How many times does the '*' print?
<pre>int b = 4;
do
\{
	cout << '*';
	b = b + 1;
\} while (b < 7);
</pre>	{
	=3
	~2
	~4
	~7
	~6
	}

<pre>int f = 40;
do
\{
	cout << '*';
	f = f + 5;
\} while (f < 61);
</pre>	{
	=5
	~4
	~6
	~1
	~7
	}

<pre>int j = 3;
do
\{
	cout << '*';
	j = j * 2;
\} while (j <= 24);
</pre>	{
	=4
	~3
	~5
	~1
	~Around a couple billion
	}

</pre>	{
	=8
	~3
	~2
	~6
	~9
	}

<pre>int i = 69;
do
\{
	int j = 35;
	do
	\{
		cout << '*';
		j = j + 5;
	\} while (j <= 50);
	i = i - 10;
\} while (i > 40);
</pre>	{
	=12
	~4
	~3
	~10
	~16
	}
